<div id="review_95015318" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/95015318" />
    <a title="Leah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3050338-leah"><img alt="Leah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474253068p2/3050338.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/95015318?book_show_action=true">Mar 20, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Leah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Leah" href="/user/show/3050338-leah">Leah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3050338-leah?shelf=adult-lit">adult-lit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3050338-leah?shelf=m-f">m-f</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3050338-leah?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer95015318&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer95015318" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2575948679898295618">Dance with the Devil is the fourth book in Sherrilyn Kenyon's Dark-Hunter series and, in my opinion, has to be one of the best of the series. In this book, we get to see more than just the surly, hateful side of Zarek; we get to see his pain, his hurt, and all the love and tenderness he is capable of. In this book, both Artemis and Dionyous have condemned Zarek to death, calling out everyone they can to kill him. Acheron, however, is able to convince Artemis to have one of Themis' justice nymphs</span>
  <span id="freeText2575948679898295618" style="display:none">Dance with the Devil is the fourth book in Sherrilyn Kenyon's Dark-Hunter series and, in my opinion, has to be one of the best of the series. In this book, we get to see more than just the surly, hateful side of Zarek; we get to see his pain, his hurt, and all the love and tenderness he is capable of. In this book, both Artemis and Dionyous have condemned Zarek to death, calling out everyone they can to kill him. Acheron, however, is able to convince Artemis to have one of Themis' justice nymphs judge him. So they send in Astrid. Blind for two weeks so Z's looks could not affect her impartiality, Astrid takes Zarek in and pushes all his buttons in order to make a decision about him. Throughout their time together, she starts to learn about him and the pain, humiliation, degradation, loneliness he has had to suffer through his whole life; she falls in love with him, and even though he doesn't admit it until she's gone, Zarek falls in love with her, too. In the end, Astrid acquits him and declares him fit to be around people, fit to live. Finally, with Ash's help, Zarek is able to realize that he deserves love, too, and goes to Astrid. She turns him into a demigod and they live happily ever after.<br /><br />Now, throughout basically the whole of this series, I have not read the books in order. Before I read Dance with the Devil, I already loved Zarek. I love the cold, acerbic, scarred characters more than anything else because they are the ones who often need the most love and care; they are the hardest to reach and often the gentlest person once you do breach their barriers. Zarek would definitely fall into this category. His extremely brutal past evokes the deepest kind of sadness in me and at some points I almost cried for the pain he had to suffer; in many ways, he reminded me of Acheron, or even Zsadist from the Black Dagger Brotherhood series. Z survived through such a horrific life, so who could blame him for being surly and hesitant to trust, to love. Once the gentle feminine hand of Astrid touched him, though, he was lost and she saved him. She showed him the loving, yet ferocious, man he could be. At the end of this book, Zarek remains one of my favorite characters from the series and he'll always have a special place in my heart.<br /><br />Astrid was an interesting character. I found her highly amusing a lot of the time, and I loved how gentle and sweet she was with Zarek. She could see the real him and didn't give up when the going got tough. She gave him the one thing she had given no man at the risk of losing everything she had: her virginity. She gave Zarek something special, something all his own, and she stood by him even when he was trying to send her away.<br /><br />Simi, always an interesting character to me, was once again one of my favorite things about this book. I love the little demon and how she just goes off on random tangents when she talks. Her devotion to Ash always succeeds in warming my heart and endearing her to me even more than her humor.<br /><br />I want to kill Artemis. I really do. I really, really wish that Ash could just let the Simi eat the bitch-goddess and be done with it already. She does nothing that does not benefit herself and never considers how she hurts Acheron or anyone else. And it was really pissing me off that she was calling Simi "it." She has a name! So I was very happy when Ash finally told her off and demanded she stop calling Simi "it." The parts with her are always the worst parts of the Dark-Hunter books for me, though. I cannot stand the time that Ash has to spend with her. It's even more horrible when I have to read about Ash and Artemis having sex. I literally cringe and read those parts as fast as I can because I cannot stand that Acheron has to lower himself to that level for his Dark-Hunters and to get sustenance.<br /><br />I have to say that I honestly thought that Sundown was trying to kill Zarek in the beginning. I guess I should have been able to figure out that he was just playing the Squires and that Ash had sent him, but I just didn't. So I was relieved to get into Jess' point of view and see the truth. Even if he wasn't a great character, I would have loved him because of his defense and protection of Zarek.<br /><br />Dance with the Devil was a fantastic book, and if there was an option of giving it even more than five stars, I would. This has got to be one of Sherrilyn Kenyon's best books to date, in my opinion, and I would read it over and over again.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2575948679898295618" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/157344371?book_show_action=true">Feb 24, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa Kay" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa Kay" href="/user/show/2459470-lisa-kay">Lisa Kay</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer157344371" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9677446815246996021"><blockquote>
  <i> This is how Italians envision Zarek of Moesia. Yum. And let me tell you, his love words to Astrid, “la mia stella” (my star)... ahhh... they sound much sexier in Italian.</i>
  <br/>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1487994829p8/1839455.jpg' height='200' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote>★★★½✩ Okay. This was a good read. By that I mean well written and a well developed world setting. It is just that it is pretty depressing reading about all the abuse Zarek suffered through-out his lifetime. Especially as a child. He was feared and rejected – for the most part unfairly – over and over. And for centurie</span>
  <span id="freeText9677446815246996021" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i> This is how Italians envision Zarek of Moesia. Yum. And let me tell you, his love words to Astrid, “la mia stella” (my star)... ahhh... they sound much sexier in Italian.</i>
  <br>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1487994829p8/1839455.jpg" height="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote>★★★½✩ Okay. This was a good read. By that I mean well written and a well developed world setting. It is just that it is pretty depressing reading about all the abuse Zarek suffered through-out his lifetime. Especially as a child. He was feared and rejected – for the most part unfairly – over and over. And for centuries! <br><br>I really like the heroine, Astrid, a Justice Nymph. (And Zarek, for that matter.) She is sent to judge Zarek for his past offences. I think I identify with my heroines more than other readers. **shrugs** I don’t know. Anyway, she takes <i>Idios,</i> a serum that allows her to not only see what Zarek endured, but to <u>feel</u> what he felt in the past, in order to better understand him. There were so many injustices, from both “friends” and family, as well as enemies. All the things were just too much for me. And the bad guy in this one doesn’t see his culpability in all that happened. I kept wanting – and waiting for Zarek to verbally stand up to him, not just physically fight him. But then, sociopaths will never admit they did anything wrong… that’s really true to life. **sigh** <br><br>There is a lot of focus on the other characters in this world (which is not a bad thing, unless you want the romance to move forward faster): Acheron, the leader of the Dark-Hunters; Artemis, as the Dark-Hunters’ primary goddess. Acheron and Artemis have a weird (twisted) relationship, which I am sure will be revealed little by little though-out this series. <br><br>I definitely need to read a happy book now. Really happy.</span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1376429955?book_show_action=true">Aug 28, 2015</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1376429955" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5295926779900863115">There are already tons of reviews with significant information about the plot so I will try to be brief.<br/><br/>I loved the hero Zarek. I feel pain and sorrow thinking about his life both before and after he became an immortal. The facts of his life are HORRIBLE. It is not possible to not be affected by it. So this is not an easy book to read. I will say that this did not make me cry. It made me rage! I wanted to hurt something/someone. I found myself taking long walks to work off some steam. I was not </span>
  <span id="freeText5295926779900863115" style="display:none">There are already tons of reviews with significant information about the plot so I will try to be brief.<br /><br />I loved the hero Zarek. I feel pain and sorrow thinking about his life both before and after he became an immortal. The facts of his life are HORRIBLE. It is not possible to not be affected by it. So this is not an easy book to read. I will say that this did not make me cry. It made me rage! I wanted to hurt something/someone. I found myself taking long walks to work off some steam. I was not satisfied that those who did him wrong got theirs. Which makes me ragey going into future books. Frankly, I am annoyed by Asheron. He subjugates himself to that bitch whore Artemis and others pay the price, like Zared. The ending scene with them made me want to puke. I am not having warm and fuzzy feelings towards him anymore.<br /><br />Astrid was awesome. She was probably the perfect match for Zared. She took some drastic measures to help him, but I was on board.<br /><br />Simi is just the best character! I need to have my own Simi! Who would not want a baby dragon demon of their own?! Playing "this little piggy" on her toes....Plus she hates the bitch whore as much as I do - although she calls her the heifer goddess.<br /><br />Just about everyone else...I am pretty pissed at the lot of them because of how they treated Zared. I think only Jess and Spawn are surviving my anger right now. They were all vicious and cruel to him. Granted they were told falsehoods - thanks to Ash and Artemis. But for the assholes in New Orleans to treat him like crap after saving their asses - Totally inexcusable!<br /><br />This story is about finding truth, redemption and love. There is a lot of time spent reliving Zared's past. At some point I had enough and I felt I was being bashed over the head with the same stuff. I appreciated that Zared, while having zero self esteem and self worth, did not seek death or martyrdom. <br /><br />The romance is not so much romance as healing Zared with her acceptance and friendship, but yet it was romantic. There were lots of little moments between them that were funny and sweet. There was a lot of action and I was happy with how everything wrapped up. There were also not so many characters that I could not keep up.<br /><br />Safety Gang notes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />Hero was not a virgin but he had only rarely paid a whore<br />Heroine was a virgin<br />retelling of terrible, sickening abuse of Zarek as a child <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer170484961" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer596951384114040141"><b>Dance with the Devil</b> is the third installment in Sherrilyn Kenyon’s Dark Hunter series. I’ve really enjoyed these books because they are filled with a ton of great characters and packed with fast-paced action.<br/> <br/>In this book, we meet Zarek who is a soulless Dark Hunter responsible for protecting mankind from the Daimons that want to destroy humans. Z’s past is long and tortured and when the story commences we learn that the goddess Artemis is about to condemn him to death for crimes that go agains</span>
  <span id="freeText596951384114040141" style="display:none"><b>Dance with the Devil</b> is the third installment in Sherrilyn Kenyon’s Dark Hunter series. I’ve really enjoyed these books because they are filled with a ton of great characters and packed with fast-paced action.<br /> <br />In this book, we meet Zarek who is a soulless Dark Hunter responsible for protecting mankind from the Daimons that want to destroy humans. Z’s past is long and tortured and when the story commences we learn that the goddess Artemis is about to condemn him to death for crimes that go against his oath to protect. That is until Acheron cuts her deal and as part of the pact they bring Astrid, the nymph of justice, to observe Z and determine if he’s worthy to live or not. That’s when the action kicks up and the stakes are raised and everything that happens from page 1 to 251 is filled with fury and fire! <br /> <br />Zarek and Astrid make a great hero and heroine for this book. I admired the conditions Astrid was placed in to judge Z’s character, and the way she tested him over and over again was heart wrenching when his secrets were revealed, but also there were moments of humor and sincerity. Zarek’s back-story is pretty rough to read about, and it’s not quickly revealed. He has a lot to his past that Astrid strives to uncover, which will help her judge his character and decide his fate. <br /><br />There were great secondary characters that played pretty big roles in this book and I hope to read more about Sasha, Simi, the Fates, Jess and of course Acheron who is suddenly become one of my favorite in this series.<br /><br />As with Kenyon’s other characters, she sure likes to put them through torturous times. Luckily though, you can tell Kenyon cares for them because she never closes the pages of her books without some just reward for her H/H. All very well done and definitely a contender for top urban fantasy/paranormal series. I enjoyed it much!<br /><br /><b>Song Choice: <a>Secrets – One Republic</a> </b><br /><br />Quotes:<br /><i> “It is only with the heart that one can rightly see. What is essential is invisible to the eye.” A...<br /><br />“Hopeless implies that at one time there was hope. And that’s another word I don’t understand. Hope only exists for people who have choices.” Z...</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="596951384114040141" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_49259687" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/49259687" />
    <a title="Holly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2127955-holly"><img alt="Holly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1520179670p2/2127955.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/49259687?book_show_action=true">Mar 14, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Holly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Holly" href="/user/show/2127955-holly">Holly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">fans of the Dark Hunter series/tortured heroes</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2127955-holly?shelf=2009">2009</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2127955-holly?shelf=my-dream-men">my-dream-men</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer49259687" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2108666411991700755">5+++ Stars<br/>*All Time Favorite Book List*<br/><br/>This book inspired so many emotions for me.<br/><br/>Long before I fell in love with the King of all Tortured Heroes, Zsadist (from JR Ward's brilliant Black Dagger Brotherhood series), there was Zarek. A truly frightening lone-wolf assassian who delights in shocking and scaring the hell out of anyone who even attempts to get to know him.<br/><br/>Zarek's backstory is heartbreaking. And in fact, a lot of the flashback scenes are a bit hard to read. But that only made me love t</span>
  <span id="freeText2108666411991700755" style="display:none">5+++ Stars<br />*All Time Favorite Book List*<br /><br />This book inspired so many emotions for me.<br /><br />Long before I fell in love with the King of all Tortured Heroes, Zsadist (from JR Ward's brilliant Black Dagger Brotherhood series), there was Zarek. A truly frightening lone-wolf assassian who delights in shocking and scaring the hell out of anyone who even attempts to get to know him.<br /><br />Zarek's backstory is heartbreaking. And in fact, a lot of the flashback scenes are a bit hard to read. But that only made me love this character more by seeing the reasons he ended up being so damaged...so cold. When Astrid enters his life, she becomes his lifeline, his reason to not give in completely to the darkness. Their scenes together are not always perfect. Kenyon frustrated me with a couple of the encounters that the two of them ended up having, but it still adds up to one of the most satisfying, heart-wrenching, and beautiful stories I have ever read.<br /><br />Kenyon's dialogue here, shines. Some of the things that Zarek says to Astrid were heartbreakingly beautiful and romantic. In my opinion this is SK's best work, and Zarek is a character that I will never forget.<br /><br />*read more reviews at my blog*<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://ravingbookaddict.blogspot.com/">http://ravingbookaddict.blogspot.com/</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="2108666411991700755" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText14627598856701226663" style="display:none">There is not a rating I can give this book. It beats any expectations I had and then some! <br /><br />My heart ached, bled, &amp; cried for Zarek. I don't think I have read another character so tormented and abused as him. I wanted to throw my hands into the book and wrap him up around me. <br /><br />He was hard done by, by a lot of people but he still cared in his way. Still put everyone's else needs before his.<br /><br />I adored Astrid, I honestly could not fault her nor could I fault this book. <br /><br />Oh and the introduction to Jess was fantastic! I cant wait to read his story!<br /><br />I really hate Artemis and think Simi does need to BBQ her!<br /><br />This story will forever be one of my favorites! <br /><br /></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('fyT8Qc4LG6S9HnTCPNL8PeGmI2YW3ap7zIMGzVLArX1IoFQrJ7pHToyO5DzRyJxRa9vec/gLBuoEflhjchBVjw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('qx+oyBGQDUHYTT3h4+SrtGhFbjsPa/3/7u8Dfs4XxuicmwCi+CFRq+ndrR8O/svY4jiTLuG9UW4mEl3Q7sc+Gg==')})
  }

With legions of fans known as Paladins (thousands of whom proudly sport tattoos from her series and who travel from all over the world to attend her appearances), her books are always snatched up as soon as they appear on store shelves. Since 2004, she had placed more than 80 novels on the New York Times list in all formats including manga and graphic novels. Her current series are: Dark-Hunters, Chronicles of Nick and The League, and her books are available in over 100 countries where eager fans impatiently wait for the next release. Her Chronicles of Nick and Dark-Hunter series are soon to be major motion pictures while Dark-Hunter is also being developed as a television series.
